# SlopScale Roadmap

> Read this at the start of every session. Update it before closing.
> Current date: 2026-06-14.

## 🔭 Host-release overlap sweep (STANDING RITUAL — run on every new Slopsmith release)

SlopScale keeps building things the host later ships (v0.2.9 shipped a Tuner, Drums, Minigames XP, NAM Rig Builder, settings export, wake-lock — we'd hand-built our own of all six). The per-feature HOST CHECK fires once at design time and can't catch a clean build *becoming* a double-build when the host later ships parity. So: **when a new Slopsmith Desktop/host release lands, do a ~15-min overlap sweep** (this is the standing counterpart to the per-feature HOST CHECK in CLAUDE.md rule 4):
1. Read the host release notes → list new capabilities.
2. Cross-check each against the **watchlist** below (our shell features the host might ship). For every overlap, make ONE call: **migrate-to-borrow** (host's is now good enough — retire ours) · **keep-ours-with-a-written-reason** (e.g. our tuner is target-aware + contained-playback-scoped) · **defer**.
3. Re-verify our borrows still work on the new build: `SLOPSMITH_SOURCE=bundled npm test` (tests our `main` against the actual user runtime) + an eyeball launch.

**Watchlist — shell capabilities we OWN that the host might ship (flip to borrow when host parity arrives):**
tuner (ours = target-aware) · drums (ours = synth/WAF, no host bank to borrow live) · XP/progress (ours = competency-typed; host = flat sqrt-score → DON'T feed; host-subscribes-to-our-emit is the on-mission path) · mixer (ours = per-instrument buses; host mix-plane is plugin-output-level + player-gated) · wake-lock · settings export · NAM tone (host borrow now GREEN — runtime-only, never vendor) · scoring/detector (host territory — we never build DSP) · asset-serving (host generic asset route exists; low-value migrate).
> The slopsmith-host-expert + devops agents carry the live version of this watchlist in their memory. Full v0.2.9 audit: project memory `project_host_release_v029_audit`.

## Session log (most recent first)

### ⏸️ STOPPED HERE (2026-06-14 session #35) — **JAM TRANSPORT: seamless A-B loop + the IN-PLACE hot-swap BUILT + verified. CORRECTS the prior session's "T11 host-blocked" call. UNCOMMITTED on slopscale-dev.** Christian: *"attempt [the hot-swap]. I also want the jam selections to loop perfectly — right now they stutter a bit when they start over."* Both done.
> **THE CORRECTION (owned):** last session I closed T11 as HOST-BLOCKED (the borrowed 3D Highway "owns its own scene lifecycle"). WRONG. Reading the `highway_3d` internals shows `draw(bundle)`/`update(bundle)` RE-READ the bundle EVERY frame with identity-keyed merge caches (`_mergeCacheChordsRef === bundle.chords`), and SlopScale's own `drawOnce` passes `rendererBundle||activeBundle` to `renderer.draw(vb)` each frame — so a live bundle SWAP is picked up next frame with NO re-init. The hot-swap is buildable on OUR side; no host API needed. (This same contract is the HOST CHECK answer below.)
> **BUILD 1 — seamless A-B loop (the "stutter" fix).** Two loop paths existed: the rolling-window chunk scheduler (GAPLESS — pre-schedules the next lap on the same ctx clock, the visual clock phase-carries) used by the whole-chart loop, vs the A-B segment loop (Jam) which did `stopAudio()`+`schedulePreviewAudio` at EVERY wrap = a ~200 ms re-schedule gap = the stutter. Fix: the A-B loop now rides the SAME gapless path — `scheduleNextChunk`/`scheduleCurrentPassAndAnchor` are loop-aware (wrap B→A, bound the window at B), `tick()`'s A-B branch calls `maybeScheduleLoopAhead` every frame + phase-carries the clock (`currentPracticeTime −= (B−A)`), and `setSegmentLoop`'s playing-branch uses the chunk scheduler so a loop set mid-play stays gapless. `stopAudio()` is GONE from the wrap. (Bonus: Workout section-loops are seamless now too.)
> **BUILD 2 — in-place hot-swap (T11).** `jamHotSwapAtWrap()` (extracted `buildJamConfig()`, shared with `jamPlay` so they can't drift): at a `_jamPending` wrap it rebuilds the chart from the LIVE panel, swaps `activeBundle`+`rendererBundle`, re-anchors the loop+clock to the new chart's `[lead,dur]`, reschedules audio from the downbeat — WITHOUT `stopRenderer`/`attachRenderer`/`replaceCanvas`/`init`. So no canvas churn, no ~3 s host-viz reload, no count-in reset; only the audio re-anchors (a deliberate content change can't gaplessly morph, but it's a clean downbeat re-entry vs the old full teardown). Falls back to the full `jamPlay()` if the renderer isn't alive.
> **VERIFY:** `probe-jam-transport.mjs` 15/15 (gapless invariant: `scheduledUntilCtx` stays ahead of the ctx clock at every frame incl. wraps; loop cycled ≥2×; canvas DOM node SURVIVES the swap = no rebuild; chart duration changed; playback never stopped; loop re-anchored to the new chart) → promoted to a durable `smoke-renderers` **jam-transport row** (per the per-system growth rule — `smoke-renderers` owns the transport system) + full `npm test` 18/18 (×3, non-flaky).
> **HOST CHECK: N/A** — no new shell capability; the renderer-re-reads-the-bundle-each-frame contract is EXISTING borrowed-highway behavior we consume (it's also what disproved the host-block). Core generation path untouched.
> **⏭️ NEXT = commit the Stage-3 transport batch on Christian's word → cut beta (`v0.7.24-beta.18`) → `git -C C:\Users\chris\Desktop\slopscale_beta pull` → his by-ear dogfood (does the jam loop seam sound seamless now? does a mid-jam genre/tempo change land without the rebuild jar?).** `main` untouched (beta-only). Deferred Jam telegraph refinements (live beats-to-wrap countdown + per-control ↻ dot) remain backlog.

### ⏸️ STOPPED HERE (2026-06-14 session #34) — **JAM UX REDESIGN round-table (8-agent panel) → Stage 1 (reliability) + Stage 2 (the full pane redesign) BUILT + verified + SHIPPED to beta; Stage 3 (hot-swap) DEFERRED with rationale [SUPERSEDED — the hot-swap was DISPROVEN-as-blocked + BUILT in session #35, see the top entry].** Christian chose "the whole arc." Spec: `docs/jam-ux-redesign-roundtable.md`. (Phase-1 band-realism PAUSED at beta.16 — gathering insight; this session pivoted to Jam GUI/usability.)

Now: **(A1)** a monotonic `_jamApplyToken` supersedes stale async applies (hammer test: 2 swaps <50ms apart → later wins) · **(A2)** `prewarmMixerCandidates()` warms the dropdown voices on jamPlay · **(A3)** `liveInstrumentReady` gate — never tear a good voice down for the thin oscillator fallback · **(A4)** `WAF_GM_TRIM` per-preset loudness table (twin of DRUM_PIECE_GAIN; organ 0.62 < clean 1.0) + decouple the genre `harmony.level` from a user-overridden voice = fixes "too quiet" · **(A5)** `liveSwapReschedule` ducks the backing group instead of a hard `stopAudio()` = fixes "abrupt." The mixer + band-strip share ONE `commitLiveVoiceSwap`.
> **BUILD — Stage 2 (the DECLUTTER), verified 18/18 + shot:** **picker** — the 29-chip wall → `renderJamStyles` rebuilt as **search + 6 collapsible families (active auto-open) + a Recent row** (~11 visible vs 29; the SAVED style id is now the source of truth via `currentJamStyleId`, so `jamPlay`/`jamPanelState`/`jamArmFromDrill` no longer read a maybe-hidden `.active` chip). **Pane** — restructured into a PRIMARY block (Style · Your band · optional aim/intent · ▶ Jam, no scroll) + collapsible **"Set up the band" / "While you play" / "More"** `<details>` (setup-vs-live, native host idiom). **Highlight** = a scaffold LADDER (most-support→bare). **Band strip** — each player's voice is now a **per-row swap menu** (`renderBandStrip` selects writing `mixerState` through `commitLiveVoiceSwap`) so changing a tone no longer means leaving for the Mixer. **Telegraph** — a `flashJamApplied()` landed-flash at the wrap (+ the existing pending chip). **Killed the green** active-state on jam controls (mirror-not-judge → `--ss-accent`). All `ss-*` CSS, host hex (no Tailwind classes). Codified the IA pattern as `docs/design-system.md` **principle #9** (the standing fix for the Custom/Workout panes too).
> **Stage 3 — (T11) hot-swap HOST-BLOCKED (closed) [⚠ SUPERSEDED session #35 — the host-block was WRONG; the highway re-reads the bundle each frame, so the swap needs no host API. BUILT — see the top entry]; (T12-apply Custom + Workout) BUILT + verified.** **(T11) in-place hot-swap → HOST-BLOCKED [later disproven].** Reading attachRenderer/startPlayback/drawOnce showed the seam is the RENDERER REBUILD; `drawOnce` passes the bundle to `renderer.draw(vb)` each frame so the 2D renderers *could* hot-swap via a bundle swap, but the DEFAULT borrowed **3D Highway owns its own scene lifecycle** — a safe in-place chart swap needs a HOST API (in-place highway chart update) that doesn't exist. *[Correction: it does NOT — `highway_3d.draw(bundle)` re-reads the bundle with identity-keyed caches, so a bundle swap IS picked up without re-init. The original read missed this.]* Marginal gain (the seam is at a telegraphed boundary). CLOSED; telegraphed seam is acceptable; file a host-ask if truly-seamless genre-switch is ever wanted. **(T12-apply) Custom + Workout panes now follow design-system #9 — BUILT + verified (18/18 + shot probes):** the Custom inspector folds the setup-once **Instrument & tuning** + the less-common **More options** (harmonize/tremolo · fretMin/fretMax/bars · keyCycle) into collapsed native `<details>` matching the pane's advanced-card look; the Workout pane folds breathe/preview-audio/session-length into a **Workout options** disclosure (Program + Segments + ▶ Start stay primary). SAFE: in-place wraps of contiguous CUSTOM-ONLY / session-only blocks (no reorder of the shared surface; Pathway mode untouched); collapse does NOT disable inputs (the screen.js ~18262 disable is `.slopscale-advanced-only`-scoped; these are custom-only/by-id), FormData/by-id integrity probe-verified (collapsed cards still feed stringSetup/fretMin/keyCycle + the workout toggles). Hidden Mixer-linked inputs kept OUTSIDE the Custom disclosure. **Refinements still deferred:** the live beats-to-wrap COUNTDOWN + the per-control `↻` dot (the pending chip + landed-flash already give the queued→landed loop). **Stage 3 effectively complete** (the only un-built piece is the host-blocked hot-swap).
> **HOST CHECK:** N/A for Stage 1 (audio mechanism over the existing engine). Stage 2 followed host-expert's MIRROR verdicts (`<details>` disclosure, the picker grammar, `ss-*` CSS copying host hex — no Tailwind classes; the rule stands). No new shell capability.
> **The question (Christian):** Jam page GUI/usability — (A) on-the-fly adjustments (instrument switch / volume / settings) sometimes don't trigger, are too quiet, or need a stop+restart / re-hit before they register; (B) the Jam menu is cluttered/overwhelming (users said so even before the 29 genre chips). Redesign the sidepane + fix the live-change feel. **Panel:** ux-designer (chair) · audio-engine · sound-design · devops · slopsmith-host-expert · gamification · learning-design · market (all 8 reported; per-lane detail in each `.claude/agent-memory/<agent>/`). Second pass on `docs/jam-mode-roundtable.md` (the 2026-06-12 feature charette; J-1/J-2 shipped).
> **UNANIMOUS DIAGNOSIS — both problems share ONE root: the pane is FLAT** (≈9 co-equal control sections + a 29-chip wall in setup order, ▶ Jam at the BOTTOM; it conflates set-once config vs live knobs, the now/wrap/async timing models, and commodity vs the wedge). The flatness causes the overwhelm AND the "unreliable" feel (a set-once control that wrap-quantizes looks identical to a live knob → feels broken when it doesn't respond instantly). **Plus REAL bugs under (A):** (1) the instrument switch is buried in the MIXER with no feedback; (2) an ASYNC RACE — the mixer `change` handler (`screen.js` ~23031–23060) is async, `await awaitVoices()` (2s cap) BEFORE rescheduling, so two quick sample-voice picks resolve out of order → "select says B, plays A" (intermittent: synth voices apply instantly); (3) "too quiet" — WebAudioFont peak-normalizes each preset (sustained ≫ plucked) + the genre `harmony.level` stays on a user-overridden voice + the oscillator fallback when the preset isn't decoded; (4) "abrupt" — `stopAudio()` hard-cut + cold reschedule, no crossfade; (5) **every live change is a full `stopPlayback→generate→start` REBUILD** — the 2026-06-12 "glitch-free in-place mutation" was never built (chair's load-bearing correction).
> **THE MODEL (all lanes + host agree): "telegraph the boundary, don't fake immediacy."** Keep the musically-honest now-vs-wrap split (style swap = a NEW band → enters now on a count-in; key/feel/depth = SAME band → top of form) but TELEGRAPH both so neither reads as a bug. Unify the FEEDBACK, not the timing. (Host idiom: its own loop count-ins into the loop rather than snapping — aligning to the wrap is on-pattern.)
> **3-STAGE PLAN (owners/anchors in the doc):** **Stage 1 — RELIABILITY (the daily pain, localized bug fixes, recommended first):** A1 token-guard the apply (`_jamApplyToken` — kills the race) · A2 preload candidate voices · A3 preset-ready gate (never the thin/quiet oscillator fallback) · A4 `WAF_GM_TRIM` per-preset loudness table (twin of DRUM_PIECE_GAIN) + decouple genre `harmony.level` on a user override (fixes "too quiet") · A5 equal-power crossfade + drop `stopAudio` (fixes "abrupt") · A7 a `probe-jam-live-change` hammer+soak (no jam smoke suite today). **Stage 2 — IA REDESIGN (declutter):** three-tier SETUP-vs-LIVE disclosure (learning-design's spine) — PRIMARY = Style (6 families + Recent, not 29) + "Your band" readout (with per-row voice swap moved OUT of the buried Mixer) + optional Intent + ▶ JAM AT THE TOP; "Set up the band" cluster (Key/Tempo/Changes/Feel/Band-role); "While you play" (Highlight ladder/Intent); Advanced `▸ More` (Depth). 29-chip wall → host picker grammar (inline search + family facets reveal-on-demand + Recent + count badge, NO modal). Highlight = a scaffold LADDER (Chord→Guide→Scale→Off, absorbs the Guide toggle). Promote Intent over Depth. Per-control `↻` dot + "Band takes it at the top — ~N beats" countdown + visual landed-flash (`--ss-accent`, never green). Kill the green active-state (mirror-not-judge). Foreground the drill→Jam hand-off over the cold grid (the wedge — market's commodity→wedge INVERSION). Host-native skin (right-slide drawer + `<details>` + `role="status"`, all `ss-*` CSS copying host hex, NEVER Tailwind classes). **Stage 3 — UNIFIED seamless apply + GENERALIZE:** A6 in-place `activeBundle` hot-swap (replace the rebuild seam → one apply model, de-jars the genre switch); adopt the IA pattern (one primary + one cluster + `▸ More` + collapse-the-wall) as a standing `design-system.md` rule + roll to the Custom/Workout panes (the OTHER "overwhelming" panes — the real leverage); + a per-style prompt/call-phrase CONTENT pass (harmony + genre-idiom).
> **HOST CHECK (host-expert, 0.2.9):** MIRROR — the filter-drawer shell, the Library picker grammar (search + chips + count badge, no modal), native `<details>`, inline `role="status"` + reuse the loop-wrap count-in. BUILD — the genre→band picker + the pending-until-wrap chip (dress native) + all `ss-*` CSS (runtime plugins aren't in the host Tailwind build scan → arbitrary classes render unstyled; rule stands). Nothing on the host roadmap flips this.
> **TABLE-STAKES we currently FAIL:** play-immediately; a live change that's instant/audible/never-silent; a non-overwhelming pane. **DIFFERENTIATOR to lead with:** the Live-Change telegraph ("talk to the band, watch it land") + the drill→Jam wire + the teaching mirror + the receding Highlight scaffold. **DRIFT (hard fences):** no jam score/combo/rank/loop-counter/clock/"best take" (never backfill the leaner pane with a score), no required intent, no export-a-track, no confirmation beep, no DAW mixing-console creep.
> **✅ RESOLVED: Christian chose "the whole arc."** Stage 1 + Stage 2 BUILT + verified + shipped to beta (`v0.7.24-beta.17`). The now-vs-wrap split was kept + telegraphed (per the panel). **⏭️ NEXT = Christian's by-ear/by-eye dogfood of beta.17** (does switching feel reliable now? is the pane no longer overwhelming?); then decide whether the deferred Stage-3 hot-swap (seamless genre-switch) is worth the transport-rewrite risk, and whether to roll the IA pattern (design-system #9) out to Custom/Workout.

### ⏸️ STOPPED HERE (2026-06-13 session #33) — **GENRE-BAND REALISM round-table (12-agent panel)** → a 3-stage "best-in-class without loops" plan + **the ROOT-CAUSE PROOF SLICE BUILT + verified + SHIPPED to beta (`03db08c` on slopscale-dev, pushed; beta **`v0.7.24-beta.16`** cut to branch + Desktop; `main` untouched). Awaiting Christian's by-ear dogfood.** Spec: `docs/genre-band-realism-roundtable.md`. Memory [[project_genre_band_realization]].
> **BUILD (proof slice — Christian chose "root-cause proof slice first" of the 4 scope options):** the two fixes behind "every genre sounds the same," both verified, 18/18 smoke + `probe-band-realism.mjs` 8/8. **(1) The realization keystone — `wafVoice` (~16966) was articulation-DEAF:** it now takes `opts {seed, artic}` and (a) imposes a per-hit ARTICULATION ENVELOPE on the GainNode `queueWaveTable` returns (chug/stab → a percussive gate; sus/ring → natural bloom — the preset's own sustain decay was why a chug rang like a held note), and (b) a DETERMINISTIC round-robin micro-variation (±~4.5¢ detune on the source's detune param, ±~0.4 dB gain, 0–4 ms onset jitter) — porting what `sgVoice` already does for the DI guitar to the WHOLE WAF band (comp/bass/keys, all 29 genres). Wired at the comp + bass call sites; the practice `notes` voice passes NO opts → byte-identical (the grading voice stays clean). Audio-only, zero chart change, zero new nodes. **(2) Continuous metric velocity — `compHitVel` (after COMP_VEL ~7062):** the 3 flat tiers became a continuous contour (an authored accent stays the 1.0 ceiling; non-accent hits lift on the beat / dip off it, bounded [0.2,1]); deterministic. **(3) Jazz two-hand keys comp — `voiceKeysComp` (~6833), specced 2026-06-05, never built:** the "jazz piano" was the guitar shell grid (one treble stack ≥58) on a piano sound, NO left hand; now a rootless A/B voicing with a LEFT-HAND 3rd-octave voice (A-form 3-5-7-9 / B-form 7-9-3-5, alternating by bar for voice-leading), wired into the `_padComp` branch. Probe confirms jazz comp now spans MIDI 52–67 vs the control shell's 59+. **LESSON (logged):** `resolveAudioProfile` keys off `cfg.audio.profile`; `cfgAudioProfile` (recipe/voicing-style path) reads `cfg.audioProfile || cfg.audio.profile` — the keys-comp triggers through `audio.profile` (the real jazz path sets it; a probe that set only the top-level key silently missed `_padComp`). Smoke-backing-engine updated to the new velocity model (183→184). **HOST CHECK: N/A** (audio realization + voicing over existing verified engines — no new shell capability). **NEXT = Christian's by-ear dogfood on beta.16** (does the band sound less "MIDI"? does the chug gate? does jazz read like a pianist?) — commit + beta + Desktop drop already DONE. **Then finish Stage 1** (the deferred voicing-type TABLE — drop2/quartal on the harmony-bus shell + country dyad6 cell + metal ♭5 tritone cell — needs new COMP_GROOVES cells + harmony spellings, so it's a reviewed follow-on, not rushed) + `humanizeDrums` ghost-ramp; then Stage 2 (the CC0 sourcing tier).
> **The question (Christian):** "country/jazz/metal bands are still barely in the ballpark — how far can procedural band generation go (articulation, note-length, sound-shaping, sub-genres, instruments/mixes, per-genre rhythm rules), and where's the absolute line before loops / generative-AI audio?" **Panel:** country/jazz/metal-idiom + guitar/bass/piano/drum-pedagogy + audio-engine + rhythm-meter + harmony + sound-design + slopsmith-host-expert (all 12 reported; per-lane detail in each `.claude/agent-memory/<agent>/project_*best*`).
> **THE DIAGNOSIS (unanimous reframe):** the charts are RIGHT (beta.13–15 placement/lock/space landed); the gap is REALIZATION, and it's content/data not architecture — no missing subsystem. Two findings + a thin third: **(A) "the band hasn't caught up to the guitar"** — the CC0 Shinyguitar voice (`sgVoice`~5732) has producer-grade rendering (RR, velocity layers, double-track), but the rest of the band plays through `wafVoice`~16966 → a bare `queueWaveTable` (one sample/region, NO per-hit envelope, NO round-robin, and the articulation tag `ev.a` is never even passed → a chug, a stab, a let-ring are the SAME sample at a different length/volume = the "MIDI smell"). **(B) the comp VOICING vocabulary is 3 shapes** (triad/shell/power, `compTargetMidis`~7300) so EVERY jazz-family genre plays the identical 3-7-9 shell forever. **(C) variation without intent** (jazz comp varies by a uniform die-roll not the form; metal's "riff" shuffles 1-bar chugs — the fixed 2-bar riff was specced, never built). Several top items are SPECCED-AND-UNBUILT (jazz rootless A/B keys voicing 2026-06-05; the per-hit envelope layer; country next-chord walk; the `gen:'approach'` passing-chord hook reserved at ~6950).
> **THE LINE (the headline answer):** procedural note-level rendering — velocity-layered+round-robin multisamples + per-hit envelopes + slides + amp/cab + per-genre procedural reverb/saturation/glue + idiomatic voicings/voice-leading/passing-chords + a bounded CONSISTENT micro-pocket — reaches "convincing sample-library / competent session band." That IS best-in-class without loops; we're ~70% there on guitar, **~40% on the rest** (ceiling mostly UNSPENT). Beyond the line (only loops/AI, forgone ON PURPOSE): inter-note performance coupling · ensemble micro-interaction · captured room/console glue · true uncorrelated human inconsistency. **Why forgoing isn't a sacrifice:** loops/AI break (1) determinism (byte-identical chart), (2) note-addressability (the chart/grader/mirror can't target opaque audio = the USP dies), (3) the practice frame (a loop is a jukebox to play OVER, not a band to play INTO; and rhythm-meter's key finding — chasing human inconsistency destroys the steady reference, so the diminishing-returns ceiling and the practice-mission ceiling COINCIDE). The moat: a deterministic, note-addressable, fully-procedural band at sample-library realism (loop tools can't target notes; AI can't reproduce the take).
> **THE 3-STAGE PLAN (full tables + owners + file anchors in the roundtable doc):** **Stage 1 — "catch the band up to the guitar," ZERO new assets, edits to existing fns:** per-hit articulation envelope on `wafVoice` (THE keystone, helps all 29 genres) · round-robin micro-variation on `wafVoice` · continuous velocity + meter-aware accent template + ghost-ramp (`vel` is already continuous downstream & trips a harder sample layer — near-free) · fix `humanizeDrums` (random jitter ERASES the authored ghost-ramp) · `voicingType` expansion (drop2/rootlessA-B/quartal/country-dyad/metal-♭5 + the unbuilt jazz two-hand `voiceKeysComp`) · jazz form-aware weighted comp picker · metal fixed 2-bar riff cell · buss-glue compressor · sharpen the 3 `MIX_RECIPES` deltas + author flams + drop ghost level · country `vary[]` bank + metal blast cell. **Stage 2 — per-genre depth + sourcing/space (CC0 assets, the crossing point):** velocity-layered+RR sample sets (drums first, bass second — the loud-layer ceiling mix can't fix) · brush/metal kits + the 6 synth-only cymbals · per-genre reverb CHARACTER + console saturation on clean buses · strum-spread+stroke-direction · genre-conditioned voice-leading tied to the Jam guide-ghost (the named USP, half-built) · tempo/per-voice swing · note-gate/legato · country next-chord walk + cells + dyad6 · sub-genre PARAM axes (`countrySub`/`jazzFeel`/metal recipe bundles + `reharmDensity`+`voicingType` — NOT new STYLE_PALETTES) · muted "chk" transient + bass slides · pedal-steel keys glide · CC0 clean/crunch cabs. **Stage 3 — connoisseur pocket + tail (by-ear, the over-humanization cliff):** per-subdivision bounded micro-pocket (clamp ±15ms, CONSISTENT) · tempo-dependent pocket depth · engine-generated passing chords (`gen:'approach'`, "connect don't choose" = the harmonic-rhythm USP) · per-limb drum push/pull · pinch-harmonic + pick-noise transient · recipe-declared extra lanes (never global) · NAM amp borrow upgrade.
> **HOST CHECK (host-expert, runtime 0.2.9):** the ONLY borrowable audio primitive is the `nam_tone` NAM amp worklet + read-only player presets/IRs (feature-detect; A2 free; cab stays our Convolver). Multisamples / kit sounds / reverb-FX / channel-count = ALL BUILD (host ships zero asset files, exposes no plugin DSP, its own inventory lists `audio-effects` as *missing*). **Nothing on the host roadmap to wait for.** The real constraint is CPU (one NAM bus max; respect the rolling-window node ceiling as channels grow). Never-build-our-own-DSP rule confirmed DETECTION-only — does not restrict synthesis/sampling/FX.
> **OPEN DECISIONS for Christian (the forks):** (1) **scope/sequencing** — RECOMMENDED: build Stage 1 (all edits to existing fns, zero assets, biggest perceived win), dogfood by ear, THEN commit Stage 2 (the sourcing tier is the only real cost). (2) **sub-genres now or later** — recommended after the core realism lands (param axis is cheap but multiplies the by-ear surface). (3) **sample-set licensing appetite** — Stage 2 kits/cabs are CC0 curation + a clearance step (gitignore-until-cleared). **✅ RESOLVED: Christian picked "root-cause proof slice first" → BUILT + verified (see the BUILD bullet above). Sub-genres + sample-set licensing remain for after the dogfood.**

### ⏸️ STOPPED HERE (2026-06-13 session #32) — **GENRE-BAND REALIZATION P0** (country/metal/jazz now audibly DISTINCT bands) + rhythm-deepening L1/L2/L3 + Tier-2 micro-timing lean + the genre-band AUTHORING PLAYBOOK (ratified) → **beta `v0.7.24-beta.15`**. [Earlier same session: metal Lead-Over-the-Band + B1 ARRANGEMENT_RECIPES (29 genres, Waves 1–3) + REAL CAB IRs + the AMP/CAB "RIG" view → beta.9.] dev `0.7.24-dev`; `main` still v0.7.23 (beta-only). **⏭️ NEXT = Christian's BY-EAR on beta.15 (does country/metal/jazz read distinct? country≠reggae?), THEN roll the proven 3-layer recipe + the playbook's 11 dimensions out to the remaining ~26 genres (cheap data, no charette — the playbook IS the process). Do NOT start the roll-out unprompted.**
> **GENRE-BAND REALIZATION P0 (Christian's #1: "every genre sounds the same" → distinct bands; 16-agent panel, `docs/genre-band-realization-roundtable.md`).** Root cause = AUDIO REALIZATION + a persisted-override bug, NOT the recipe DATA (the recipes already differentiated). SHIPPED beta.10→.15 (`d8517bd`→`584f969` on slopscale-dev; `main` untouched), plan "prove 3 (country/metal/jazz) then roll to 29": **THE bug Christian hit** (jamPlay `Object.assign({},readConfig(),…)` inherited persisted backingComp/backingBass/backingDensity/backingPadDev → recipe ignored; fix `d456798` clears them in the jam cfg — lesson [[feedback_probes_mask_persisted_state]]); **Keys un-orphan** (`screen.js:16634` bus fix `role:'pad'`/`padBus`→Keys + `voiceBackingPad` rootless-above-comp); **per-genre AUDIO_PROFILES** (bass.tone upright country/jazz, pad, drums.kit + a `validateAudioProfiles` startup guard — also closed the never-guarded drums.kit gap); **`bass_drive` amp** (preHp~30 + noCab so it keeps the fundamental — bass-ped's catch; metal/punk overdriven bass); **`MIX_RECIPES`** delta table + `applyMixRecipe` (per-genre drum-EQ/comp on the SHARED FluidR3 + level/pan/carve/send/masterTrim); **`metal_drive`** (galloping kick — metal's groove tier was a generic rock beat); **workflow**: instant genre switch (chip click while playing → jamPlay NOW), a "Your band" lineup strip, 29 chips grouped into 6 families. Then RHYTHM-DEEPENING (Christian's by-ear "rhythms too simple / country sounds like reggae"), 3 layers: **L1 patterns** (`country_chuck` lands ON the backbeat not a chop-every-offbeat = the reggae skank; `two_feel_walk` bass root-5 + 6→♭7 walk-up; `country_backbeat` cross-stick; `metal_chug_stab` syncopated breathing riff + `root_gallop` locked to the a.nna kick); **L2 per-genre comp VOICING** (`voiceChord` `voicingStyle:'triad'` = low root-DOUBLED guitar chord, re-grab/no-voice-lead for country/folk/rock vs `'shell'` = rootless spread + voice-led for jazz/funk — keyed by `backingVoicingStyle(profileId)`/`VOICING_TRIAD` set; fixes "comp sounds jazzy"); **L3 seed-rotated variation** (comp cells may carry `vary:[grid…]`; `buildBackingEvents` rotates per-BAR bar-absolute/no-repeat/deterministic; `charleston` got 6 jazz variants → jazz comp breathes). **Tier-2 polish (`584f969`):** `FEEL_TIMING`+`applyFeelLean` per-genre micro-timing LEAN (country backbeat drags ~11ms behind the kick, metal stays tight) + `metal_chug_stab` `vary:[base,breathing,gallop]` 3-variant phrasing. **CODIFIED:** `docs/genre-band-authoring-playbook.md` — the reusable process for building/fixing ANY genre band (11 dimensions + a per-genre worksheet + neighbour-confusion bright-line tests: country≠reggae/polka/folk, funk≠disco, blues≠rock…), **ratified by country-idiom-architect** (it added Space-as-identity, Interlock-alongside-Lock, the neighbour table, load-bearing-dimensions-first) + wired into CLAUDE/AGENTS file map. 183 backing checks + 18/18; the smoke suite's stale cell-name assertions updated to the renamed cells (`c0c1da6`). Memory [[project_genre_band_realization]].

> **VERIFY (session #32, pre-build):** the distorted-comp plumbing was confirmed correct before the build — the two prior probe "FAILs" were PROBE BUGS (wrong rung `metalcore_chug` emits no comp + wrong artifact: `makeBundle` assembles `backingEvents`, not `generateExercise().chart`). That verification is what surfaced the KEY FINDING below.
> **KEY FINDING — the headline realism was CORRECT but DORMANT (now LIT by the build above).** Nothing shipped emits distorted comp: metal/djent pathways are RIFF DRILLS (`rhythm_pulse`/`pedal_riff`, anchor-based, `backingStyle:'pad'` → synth-pad backing, `compCellForConfig`→null), and `strum_comp` suppresses backing comp. The ONLY trigger is a LEAD/scale activity over a metal PROGRESSION with a comp groove (had to force it: `blues_shuffle` + override profile→djent + `backingComp`→`rock_chug`). Same dormancy for guitar `n.mt`→`sg_mutestr` (mt ghosts only come from the slap-BASS builder, and bass forces the non-DI voice) and the `chuck` samples (no `COMP_GROOVES` cell uses `a:'chuck'`). LIVE-now pieces of the changeset: shiny DI guide (shipped), distorted Keys staying synth (`pad` slot), accent-aware strum stagger.
> **DECISION (Christian, session #32): BUILD A LIVE TRIGGER FIRST — don't land dormant code.** Add a 'metal/djent LEAD over a chugging rhythm-section backing' context (the player solos while the band chugs a double-tracked DI-through-Metal rhythm guitar) so the realism actually sounds, vet with the panel, commit it all as one live feature. **HOST CHECK: N/A** (content over existing verified engines — backing comp + amp + double-track already built; no new shell capability). **Panel** (metal-idiom owns · learning-design chairs · harmony · guitar-pedagogy) ran, synthesized, BUILT — see the BUILD bullet at the top. **DONE:** committed `67a22f4` + pushed dev + beta `v0.7.24-beta.1` (branch + Desktop). **NEXT:** Christian dogfoods the beta (clean lead over the double-tracked metal comp + the open amp-preset gates); when happy → promote dev→main + version-bump (`plugin.json` + `SLOPSCALE_VERSION` → `0.7.24`) + tag + GitHub release.

### ✅ (2026-06-09 session #23 cont.) — GRADING P0 RE-FIX (sustained/DI playing now scores) — COMMITTED `da0d6ef` + beta cut to Desktop (v0.7.14-beta.1)
> Christian: "grading still isn't working in SlopScale but it IS in Slopsmith." **The 2026-06-08 rebuild over-corrected** — it mirrored the host silence gate but ALSO added a +11dB per-note ONSET requirement the host never had. Diagnosis: **slopsmith-host-expert ×2** (confirmed against the pinned note_detect **1.10** consumer): the host's gate (`note_detect` :5550-5588) is a **pure ONE-WAY VETO** — runs only on an already-`detected` pitch verdict, forces a miss over ±200ms iff samples present AND peak `inputLevel < 0.02`, SKIPS when no samples ("no telemetry ≠ silent"), **NO onset anywhere**. On a high-gain/compressed/sustained **DI** the level envelope is flat → a re-pick is only a few dB over the ringing baseline → no onset fires → **every note after the first was rejected**. The synthetic-pluck e2e + web-analyser test path hid it.
> **FIX (`da0d6ef`, 16/16):** `ptCreditGatePasses` now mirrors the host EXACTLY — dropped `ptOnsetIn` + the `rest×4` floor inflation + the whole onset/baseline/warm-up/calibration machinery; a one-way level veto at **fixed 0.02**, skip-when-no-samples (`ptHasSamplesIn`). `_lvlPushSample` = a sample ring + `_ptHadInput` arming. The sub-0.02 idle-residual false-positive stays dead (vetoed when the meter is live). `smoke-scoring-e2e` REWORKED to 3 contexts: PLUCK (transient scores), **STEADY full-level (SUSTAINED real playing MUST score — now 13/43 A2 notes, was 0 under the onset gate)**, SUB-FLOOR 0.004 (inaudible → 0). `plugin.json` + `SLOPSCALE_VERSION` → **0.7.14-dev**. Memory `project_grading_rebuild` (regression-fix section) + host-expert `project_grading_regression_diff_2026-06-09`.
> **⚠ NEEDS CHRISTIAN'S DI-RIG DOGFOOD** — the headless e2e only drives the WEB level path; the desktop `getLevels` path (the Axe-FX DI) is confirmable only on his rig. **Beta cut to Desktop** (`cut-beta.mjs --dry-run "<Desktop>\slopscale_beta"` → `slopscale_beta` **v0.7.14-beta.1** from `da0d6ef`) for that dogfood. If still dead: log `slopsmithDesktop.audio.getLevels()` while playing — `inputLevel`~0 ⇒ the engine meter isn't live in contained playback (fix: ensure `startAudio`, or gate-inactive on a dead meter). Escalation: `createNoteDetector({highway})` drives the host's real grader (heavyweight).

> **NEW CONTENT — 19 pathways, 4 packs** (all opt-in via Pack-manager "+", family-grouped): **Bass: Scales** (`bass_scales_ladder` — one-box→two-octave→modes-in-one-shape→shifts→whole-neck; `scale`/`position_shift`/`full_neck`, position system never CAGED) · **Bass: Arpeggios** (`bass_arpeggios_ladder` — triads→7ths→inversions→over-changes) · **Bass: Groove & Right Hand** (`bass_groove_rh_ladder` — pulse→rake→16th-stamina→funk-pocket-at-speed→three-finger) · **Sweep Picking** (`concept_sweeps`, Concepts family — 3-string→5-string A-shape→roll&apex (E-shape)→7th sweeps→over-changes). Relabeled the existing `bass_foundations_ladder` "Bass"→"Bass: Foundations". SKILL_TREE_EDGES chains + FORM_CUE_RUNGS.sweep_roll_apex + 19 `<option>`s wired.
>
> **3 engine/data additions (Christian chose "all rungs first-class"):** (A1) **`sweepStrings:N`** limiter (top-N strings; anti-leak in applyPathwayConfig + hidden field) → the true 3-string entry rung. (A2) **first-class seventh sweeps** — DEVIATION FROM THE APPROVED PLAN, flagged: instead of authoring 15 seventh CAGED templates (would risk the startup finger-collision guard for no functional gain beyond static finger labels), seventh sweeps route through `sweepArpeggioPositions`, which I rewrote to **coverage-first** (bass string = root, each higher string prefers an UNCOVERED chord tone nearest the running fret) so every chord reliably rakes all 4 tones incl. the 7th — probe `lens=[4,4,4,4,4,4,4,4]`. (A3) **`rhTechMode` pulse|crossing|rake|three_finger** in `buildRightHandTechniqueExercise` (rake = descending octave→5th→root one-finger drag; +hidden field/anti-leak).
>
> **Part 2 — instrument/string/tuning (screen.js handlers + isHiddenNode):** Bug-1 FIXED — switching FAMILY now persists to the L1 store (`slopscale.instrument`) (the instrument `change` handler set `setup.value` without dispatching, so `instrumentStoreSave` never ran → reverted on reload). Bug-2 FIXED — both change handlers now `renderPathwayList()` so the picker repaints per instrument. Bug-3 (approved) — `dropPathwayIfUnplayable()` drops to Custom when the active Ladder rung can't be played on the new instrument (guided mode only). Plus **`isHiddenNode` family-match** extension: a pathway coded for the other family (its base.stringSetup) is now hidden (except instAgnostic/Rhythm) — fixes the new bass Scales/Arps packs (agnostic practice types) showing on guitar AND the symmetric latent bug (guitar pathways yanking a bass player to guitar via the stringSetup write). Plus **`applyPathwayConfig` instrument-FIRST** fix (latent, pre-existing): it now switches the instrument class before writing `practiceType`, so a bass-native rung (right_hand_technique etc.) no longer silently falls back to `scale` when the practice-type `<option>` is disabled (bit when restoring a bass pathway on reload / selecting from a guitar context).
>
> **Verified:** `npm test` **16/16** (after every engine change; 120/120 generators) + `probe-sweep-bass-ladders.mjs` **28/28** (sweepStrings→3 strings, 7th sounds on every chord, rake crosses strings vs pulse single-string, all 19 pathways generate, family-switch persistence, drop-to-Custom, picker repaint per instrument). Startup guards (no-unison, pack-integrity, applicability) green on load.

### ⏸️ STOPPED HERE (2026-06-08 session #18) — BACKING STEP 5 + version badge SHIPPED to `slopscale-dev` (pushed); Desktop install now a GitHub clone
> Work on **`slopscale-dev`** (the WIP branch; `main` = published releases). **Backing-engine step 5** per the approved plan `.claude/plans/proud-swinging-codd.md` (4-agent panel: drum-pedagogy + rhythm-meter + jazz-idiom + sound-design). **The headline fix: a jazz trio no longer plays under a rock drummer** — a swung jazz cfg now rides a real spang-a-lang ride instead of `straight_8th_rock` (the biggest remaining swing mis-teach). What landed:
> - **Step 0 — voice rename to the host `lib/drums.py` PIECES vocabulary** (snake_case): `hatClosed→hh_closed`(42) `hatOpen→hh_open`(46) `hatPedal→hh_pedal`(44) `crash→crash_l`(49) `tomHi/Mid/Lo→tom_hi/mid/low`; ADDED `snare_xstick`(37) `tom_floor`(41) `ride_bell`(53) `crash_r`(57) `china`(52) `splash`(55) `bell`(80). A SlopScale drum event now maps 1:1 onto the host's 18-piece kit. Renamed across `ACOUSTIC_PIECES`/`DRUM_CORE_PIECES`/`DRUM_GROOVES`/`chokeOpenHats`/`buildGenericDrumGroove`/`DRUM_NATURAL_DUR`/`scheduleDrumHit`/`scheduleSynthDrumHit`.
> - **Step 1 — schema:** per-lane `{pat,vel,div}` (quiet kit + a 16th double-kick under an 8th hat); tokens `x`=feathered/whisper · `o`=open-hat (→hh_open) · `f`=flam (grace+main); `cellBars` (multi-bar clave); `preSwung` swing-lock; **`FILLS` registry** + `fillFamily`/`fillEveryBars` (default 8) — a fill swaps the phrase's last bar, mutes the time-keeping hats, drops a `crash_l` on the next downbeat; **`comp[]`** seed-rotated jazz snare overlay; **`DRUM_PIECE_GAIN`** per-piece relative gain (ride 0.5 / foot 0.3 / snare 1.0 — applied in BOTH drum engines, tames the hot GM ride).
> - **Step 2 — 8 grooves:** `jazz_swing` (spang-a-lang ride + hi-hat foot 2&4 + feathered kick + comp[], NO backbeat snare) · `reggae_one_drop` · `funk_16th` · `metal_double_kick` (per-lane div:4 double-bass) · `train_beat` · `gospel_pocket` · `bossa` (2-bar clave) · `second_line` (2-bar). Kept the original 4 (lanes renamed).
> - **Step 3 — routing:** `resolveGroove` is style-keyed (`GROOVE_FOR_PROFILE` jazz→jazz_swing) and reads the profile from BOTH `cfg.audioProfile` and `cfg.audio.profile` (`cfgAudioProfile`). **Deliberately does NOT route a bare `swing:'swing'`→jazz** (jazz-idiom). Added `audioProfile:'jazz'` to the two swung jazz pathways that lacked it (`vl_connect`, `ii_V_I_workout`). Drumless via opt-in `cfg.drums:'none'` (NOT by token — `bluegrass` is shared by country, which has a drummer).
> - **Step 4 — seeded humanization** (`humanizeDrums`, salt `^0x4452554d` so it never correlates with the bass roll): ±3–8 ms micro-timing + velocity jitter, baked before swing, the loop's "one" protected (no flam vs the wrap), electronic kits ×0.2 (machines are tight). **Determinism is a hard rule** (same cfg ⇒ byte-identical events).
> - **Step 5 — synth voices** for the new lanes (`ride` warm tip / `ride_bell`+`bell` / `snare_xstick` woody / `hh_pedal` dark foot / `tom_floor` / `crash_r`/`splash`/`china`). **`SAMPLED_DRUM_NOTES` gate**: the 7 new pieces have no committed FluidR3 one-shot → they take the synth voice instead of a per-hit 404 (loadWafPreset retries on 'failed'). The core kit (kick/snare/hats/toms/ride/crash_l/hh_pedal) still plays SAMPLED.

### ✅ Rhythm-ladder genre-spanning expansion — DESIGNED + Batch 1 BUILT, uncommitted (2026-06-04)
> **~23-agent group-design session** (learning-design CHAIR + rhythm-meter engine + guitar/bass/drum-pedagogy + **18 genre/subgenre idiom lanes**: metal/punk/surf/blues/jazz/funk/latin/reggae/afrobeat/bluegrass/country/gypsy-jazz/new-orleans/norteño/tango/flamenco/disco/prog). Mandate (Christian): expand `concept_rhythm` from 6 rungs into a **full genre-spanning transferable rhythm curriculum**, absorbing the queued gallop + single-string build-out. **Full spec + per-cell math + decision log: `docs/rhythm-ladder-roundtable.md`; durable synthesis: memory `project_rhythm_ladder_design`; per-lane detail in each `.claude/agent-memory/<agent>/`.**
> **Architecture (load-bearing, unanimous):** ONE genre-NEUTRAL **~11-rung spine** (A·Grid: Subdivisions/16th-Pocket · B·Feel: Swing&Shuffle/Displacement + NEW **Gallop&Snap**/**Accent Displacement** · C·Pulse-Frame: NEW **Single-String Pulse**[keystone=1 note,palm-mute,low string]/**Half-Double-Time**[goal-card]/Odd-Meters · D·Two-Pulses: Over-the-Barline/Metric-Mod[gated]/Polymeter[gated] · Capstone **Trade-Bars/Make-a-Groove**). A genre's device attaches ONLY as a `vary[]` step, an app rung in its OWN Style pack, or goal-card prose — **NEVER a new band rung** (the anti-bloat rule, same as the chord ladder).
> **Substrate = a `RHYTHM_CELLS` data table** (`fillNotesFromSeq`'s `steps[]` path already tiles bar-commensurate cells → the Latin/dotted/gallop/clave wave is CURATION not code) + an `assertRhythmCellsValid` startup guard (every cell sums to whole bars — caught a bad Scotch-snap). **tresillo `[3,3,2]` = the cross-idiom atom** (Latin/NOLA/tango/norteño point at one def); clave/habanera/afrobeat-bell/flamenco-compás(`12/8:3+3+2+2+2`)/gallop-family all drop in as data. Honest framing: a single line teaches the TIME of a feel, never the ensemble INTERLOCK ("tap the clave's time").
> **Gated (spec'd, not near-term):** prog's NEW flag — a per-bar **changing-meter array** `meterSequence:[...]` (simpler than polymeter + more idiomatic → ELEVATE ahead of it) · the polymeter cell (Tier-3 decoupled phrase-clock + a load-bearing re-lock visual) · metric modulation (block-seam). Bass parity ≈ zero new build but the right hand diverges on 3 rungs (16th-Pocket→ghost-pocket, Gallop→pick/3-finger, Single-String→root-pulse; strip CAGED on bass).

mirrors no-unison) + `rhythmSteps` reads it · **`buildRhythmPulseExercise`** = the new `rhythm_pulse` generator (one palm-muted low-string note, the cell, a movable `pulseAccent` 0–3) → dispatch + `readConfig` `pulseAccent` + screen.html hidden input + practiceType `<option>` + 6 new subdivision `<option>`s · **5 new spine rungs** (`rhy_gallop_snap`/`rhy_accent_displace`/`rhy_single_string`/`rhy_half_double`/`rhy_trade_bars`) + the `concept_rhythm` band reordered into the 11-rung 4-strata spine + 5 pathway `<option>`s · the **tresillo + son_clave cross-idiom cells wired** (subdivision options + varys on Single-String Pulse = "tap the clave's time on one note"). **Verified:** `node --check`; ### ✅ COMMITTED — Chord Concept ladder, Phases A + B (2026-06-04)
> The **`concept_chords`** pack (Concepts family, **guitar-only**), 7 rungs over `strum_comp`, triads/grips SOUNDED TOGETHER (vs the Triads ladder's arpeggios):
> - **Phase A** (`81071d1`, pushed): **Cowboy Chords** → **The Five CAGED Shapes** → **Barre Chords** → **Comping the Changes** (triad/power). Adds `voicingPosition` (open/movable) + `strumPattern` hidden fields, read in `readConfig` + consumed by `buildStrumCompExercise`.
> - **Phase B** (the STRUM_GRIPS unlock): a **separate `STRUM_GRIPS` movable-grip table** (7th/9th/11th/13th/sus — do NOT bloat CAGED) consulted in `pickStrumGrip` before the triad fallback, so 7ths voice the 7th instead of reducing to a triad and 9/11/13 voice at all. 3 new rungs: **Sevenths Around the Neck** (min7/maj7/dom7, E+A barre forms over ii–V–I) → **The Harmonized Key** (the diatonic-7th lap `[1..7]`, incl. the dorian IV7 carrier) → **Color: 9ths, 11ths & 13ths** (funk dom9, neo-soul min9/min11, big-band dom13, sus — dom9 labelled honestly, never "11"). Startup guard `assertStrumGripsValid` machine-proves every grip's pcs ⊆ its `CHORD_FORMULAS` stack + no same-MIDI unison + no impossible finger (one finger ≠ two frets). **Reviewed: harmony-theory GO-no-fixes (ratified the fuller dom13, the auto-override modal honesty); guitar-pedagogy GO-with-fixes (3 `fg` finger-hint bugs fixed + the finger-collision guard added).** Verified: `probe-chords-b.mjs` (extensions voice ≥4 distinct pcs, not triad reductions) + `probe-chords.mjs` regression + full 13-suite `npm test` EXIT 0.
> **Phase C DEFERRED:** inversions-as-grips + the descending-bass slash token (harmony's rung 6). **Bonus unblocked:** STRUM_GRIPS now supplies the dom9/sus grips the deferred funk-dom9 + pop-sus *palette* wiring were waiting on. Memory `project_chord_concept_ladder`. **Both phases committed to `main`; Phase A pushed, Phase B local — push when asked.**

### ✅ Dev-ops e2e screen.js AUDIT + host bigger-picture refresh (2026-06-05, post-release)
> **The audit** (full report in dev-ops agent memory `project_screenjs_e2e_audit`, skill-scoped path): 2 real findings, 1 heads-up, 1 minor; everything else verified clean (error handling, host-API guards, resource hygiene, state machine, storage, injection surface).
> - **✅ FIXED same day — the "sideways stop" teardown hole:** regenerate-while-playing / leave-via-nav went through `stopRenderer()` which skipped `sessionEnd()` + `releaseWakeLock()` → the screen stayed awake forever AND an abandoned run flushed later with wiped hit/miss counts = a FAKE CLEAN PASS crediting tiers/proof-loop. Fix: `stopRenderer` now closes the session (scorer state still alive) + releases the lock when stopping mid-play. Guard PROMOTED into `smoke-renderers` ("wakelock-pair" row; the probe stays local). Net 15/15.
> - **⏭️ QUEUED (do before pushing long Workouts; pairs with the backing-engine §14 work): rolling-window audio scheduler.** Play on a 30-min Woodshed schedules EVERYTHING up front — measured 39,286 nodes / 1.57s main-thread freeze, repeating at the loop wrap mid-practice. Fix = schedule ~30–60s ahead from the frame loop (extend `maybeScheduleLoopAhead`).
> - **Noted:** the PT_HIT_FRAMES floor — notes <~80–120ms can't collect 2 frames, so 16ths above ~150–160 BPM under-score; accepted (false hit > missed hit); cheap follow-up = 1 frame for notes <100ms if dogfooding feels it. Minor: a first-load attach race can orphan a renderer (generation-counter fix, low priority).
> **The host refresh** (slopsmith-host-expert memory `project_host_refresh_2026-06-05`, skill-scoped; host = 0.2.9-beta.1 @ ca3be33): **piano is pre-WIP host-side** (viz-only plugin moved out of core; no track format; no MIDI input) — deferral stands, budget an in-tree piano-roll renderer someday. **Backing-engine intel:** `nam_tone` NO LONGER BUNDLED in core → vendor-the-worklet vs feature-detect+degrade is a Christian decision at build time (AGPL relicense bears on it; plugins exempt but curated-list needs a compatible license — SlopScale ships NO license file); the chord-event timeline = confirmed genuine build (nothing to borrow); `lib/drums.py` GM vocabulary = borrow as the drum-voice naming reference; Minigames SDK now CORE-bundled (grading reaches Desktop users). **WATCH:** the host's capability-runtime pivot (our APIs are tracked compat bridges; the upcoming `note-detection` capability formalizes our #254 gems hook — now pinned by a host test), a future viz registry (highway_3d borrow). **DEV-OPS FOLLOW-UPS:** the Desktop install is repackaged (Electron asar) → `launch.ps1`'s `bundled` mode is DEAD (fix/retire) + #650 Stage-2 unverifiable from disk + the SessionStart gate hook checks a path that no longer exists (update/retire the hook).

### ✅ Real-audio scoring e2e PROVEN → PROMOTED → and it caught a REAL grader bug, FIXED (2026-06-05, post-release)
> Christian challenged "have you tested the tuner/grading hooks with Slopsmith?" — honest answer was NO (smoke-gems injects a FAKE scorer by design; nobody had played real audio at the real detector). Built the real test: a synthesized 110 Hz A2 WAV streamed via Chromium's fake-mic flags → the HOST's real detector → the meter reads "A2" → grading lights `hit` → accuracy counts. ALL PASS — note detection genuinely works on current Slopsmith.
> - **PROMOTED per the dev-ops consult → `smoke-scoring-e2e.mjs`** (suite #15; a genuinely new SYSTEM — the only real-audio test). Consult verdict implemented in full: SDK-absent host = hard-FAIL with a named message (a skip would swallow the #1 thing the suite catches); WAV → tmpdir + per-PID + unlink; WEIGHTS entry; added to `test:seq` (run-all glob-discovers, the chain is hand-maintained); console-error capture with NO benign list (scoring failures ARE the point); bundle stashed once; **a negative control** (same tone, drill re-keyed to D → no `hit` allowed). Net = **15/15 at 17.4s** (fits in renderers' shadow). Dev-ops memory `project_mic_e2e_promotion`.
> - **⭐ The negative control caught a REAL grader bug on its first run:** the detector's lock-on SWEEPS from startup garbage through the ±50¢ window (measured: +4023¢ → +485¢ → −285¢ converging on a −500¢ wrong note) and the single-frame grader permanently scored the false frame — every drill's FIRST note could false-hit, inflating the proof-loop's clean-run gate. **FIXED (`ptOnPitch`): `PT_HIT_FRAMES = 2` consecutive in-tune frames (~80ms) required to score**; streak resets on out-of-tune/start/stop. Verified: e2e positive still hits, negative clean, full net green.
> - **Small slice (logged):** the accuracy readout can momentarily show hits > passed ("2/1 (200%)") — `_ptScored.size` vs `passedTotal` counting drift in `ptOnPitch`; cosmetic (the suite WARNs, doesn't gate). Related 30-min check: confirm the proof-loop verdict does NOT share this inflatable counter.
> - **Mic-permission affordance DOWNGRADED to small-polish** (was flagged urgent): the e2e proved the pitch meter IS a visible on-state signal and the browser prompts on first play; the only gap is the denied/failed state (meter silently absent, no retry). Zero-code mitigation = a line in the v0.7.3 Discord thread ("no meter = browser blocked the mic").
> - **DECISION (Christian, 2026-06-05): the next BIG slice = the BACKING ENGINE** (docs/backing-engine-roundtable.md) — chosen over piano/drums ("Def backing engine"; piano is still WIP host-side anyway). A slopsmith-host-expert bigger-picture refresh (host piano status, borrowable backing capabilities, host direction) ran the same day — see its agent memory.

### ✅ DECISION (2026-06-03) — STAY A PLUGIN, do NOT register as a Slopsmith minigame
> Christian's reframe (host plain *plugins* look utilitarian; SlopScale's contained player + four-mode shell + gamified progression *feel* more "minigame-like") went to a **5-agent panel** (slopsmith-host-expert → gamification + market + learning-design + ux). **Unanimous: stay a plugin.** Verdicts in each agent's `.claude/agent-memory/`.
> **The deciding fact (host-expert, verified vs checkout 0.2.9-alpha.7):** a Slopsmith "minigame" is NOT a higher tier or a separate prestige section — it's a `minigame` block + `register()` that drops you into a **host-owned single-round HARNESS** (modifier-picker modal → host stage + a host **Quit** button → play ONE round → the *host's* score/Play-Again results modal; navigate-away = force-teardown). That's a **lower-altitude** container than our four-mode app, and the host runSummary modal would **hijack our proof-loop summary**. Host gamification is shallow (flat global XP + a **local-only** best-score leaderboard + XP-threshold unlocks; **no streaks/achievements/competency model**) → **nothing on the progression side to borrow** that would save building our own; our proof-loop + Depth Ladder is strictly richer.
> **Per lane:** gamification — host best-score board = exactly the score/rank dark pattern we cut; market — a games-hub tile **buckets us with novelty toys** + cheapens the serious-tool identity, and discoverability isn't our binding constraint (self-hosting friction + the proof readout + word-of-mouth are); learning-design — a single round can't hold a ladder or a multi-block Workout, and "score" framing nudges mastery→performance goals; ux — category error, the round stage fights a persistent multi-mode workspace.
> **The "feed host XP/leaderboard WITHOUT registering" hybrid (endpoints ARE callable w/o `register`): DEFERRED** — buys ~nothing now (no hub tile without the manifest; XP is a meaningless 2nd currency; a best-score feed fights our competency readout). IF ever taken: feed **competency events (clean-rung verdicts) not rounds/time**, one-way, **invisible in our UI**, decorative-never-load-bearing.
> **Instead (cheap, on-mission):** (1) stay a plugin — keep nav screen + four-mode shell + contained playback (zero work); (2) earn "first-class" by craft — a sharper **practice/verb-framed nav label + a distinct nav icon** + a strong first-paint mode-overview identity (queued with slopscale-ux-designer); the **proof card** is the outward discoverability hook, not a hub tile; (3) the one good idea the round model surfaced — a **capstone "test"/Score-Attack layer** is pedagogically legit, but build it INSIDE our player at the top of a rung's arc crediting a competency (the proof-loop already aspires to this), never via the host harness; (4) north-star guardrail added to CLAUDE/AGENTS: *gamification describes mastery, never substitutes a score for it.*

Also deferred: the drill side reading `chart.timeline` (Connect Stage 2); the unified chart schema (midi spine + str/key/voice addenda) for piano/drums; `applyPathwayConfig` stringSetup-respect + caged→position adapt; vocal. **Defer (needs generator):** Modal Color (bright-modal generator), the Playing-the-Changes "approach" rung (the chord-event timeline). **Open decision for Christian:** whether to RE-HOME the existing single-concept pathways (`guide_tones_path`/`seventh_vocab`/`ii_V_I_workout`/`bend_drill`/`whole_neck_freedom`/`sweep_arpeggio_primer`) into their ladders (cleaner; removes them from Core bands) vs the current additive duplication. See the "Backing-Engine Rebuild" section below.

## 🎚️ Backing-Engine Rebuild — DESIGNED 2026-06-03 · **plan v2 LOCKED + BUILD STARTED 2026-06-05**

Full charette on the **chord-progression + backing-track + harmony/metric** engines: *make it
better per-genre + more lifelike; what's the USP.* Panel = harmony-theory (chair) + rhythm-meter +
sound-design + audio-engine + drum-pedagogy + market + learning-design + bass/piano-pedagogy + **25
genre lanes** (shoegaze/surf/emo/punk held out as texture/lead-only). **Full spec + per-genre
signature table + decision log: `docs/backing-engine-roundtable.md`; durable synthesis: memory
`project_backing_engine_roundtable`.**

**2026-06-05: an 11-lane panel re-check (the build-owning lanes, background agents) re-validated the
spec against everything shipped since — synthesis + locked decisions in the doc's "Build-plan v2"
addendum** (per-lane detail in each agent's `.claude/agent-memory/<agent>/project_backing_*`).
Plan-changers: the timeline keystone is **~40% already shipped** (`compileChordTimeline` exists,
backing + proof metric read it — step 1 shrinks to finishing it + two per-block assembly fixes);
**one cell grammar** (COMP_GROOVES = the STRUM_PATTERNS grid with object steps; RHYTHM_CELLS = the
shared timing atoms via a `cellOnsets` bridge); the **rolling-window scheduler is step 0**
(unanimous); articulation costs **zero extra nodes** (automation on the WAF-returned GainNode);
mix 7a (velocity tiers + ARTIC envelopes) ships **inside** step 3; backing bass lands **ROOT on 1**
kick-locked (flip of Connect's guide-tone preference); drums rename to the host `lib/drums.py`
vocab; seeded determinism baked at generation (byte-golden charts). **Christian's locked decisions:**
(1) **build all ~9 taught genres BEFORE release** (overrides the panel's ship-one-and-measure rec);
jazz = the vertical pilot through steps 3–5, blues = the A/B control; (2) **NAM = in-house
WaveShaper + CC0 cab-IR chain + feature-detect `nam_tone`** (NO vendoring — upstream is unlicensed;
follow-ups: clear a CC0 IR + add our repo LICENSE); (3) **proof-loop flag ON with this build**;
(4) minors per panel rec: REF_TRIM fader-unity defaults, funk goes Dorian, pushed landings credit
the seam proof, `backingDensity` authored-only, A/B pad-vs-comp toggle = dev flag.

**Diagnosis:** the harmony is right (`COMMON_PROGRESSIONS` + the `voiceChord` engine are good); the
whole **rhythm/texture layer is missing**. Backing = exactly TWO comp shapes — one sustained voiced
**pad/bar** + the **blues boogie** — harmony **bar-locked**, backing **bass = the pad's sustained
root**, **4 drum grooves**, **one global swing**. So every non-blues genre plays *a held chord over a
rock backbeat*. Fix = recombinable **PRIMITIVES**, NOT 30 canned palettes (north star).

**USP (market):** the backing is a **teaching instrument wired to the drill + the fretboard mirror**,
not an accompaniment — the only loop nobody else closes (iReal accompanies/never teaches; BiaB
lifelike/inert; Chordify song-locked). **Only true differentiator = voice-leading + harmonic rhythm
tied to the Jam mirror.** Per-genre feel for already-taught genres = **table-stakes**; **30+ palettes
= sprawl/DRIFT** (this is the **#1 off-mission magnet**). **Drift bright line:** *better-PLAYING vs
better-SOUNDING-unattended* → loop a vamp NOT arrange a song; no arrangement sections; **no backing
export**; no "make me a jam" entry without a drill; Jam stays a mirror.

**KEYSTONE (unanimous) = the beat-based CHORD-EVENT TIMELINE** (chords on beats, `durBeats`,
`push`/anticipation, engine-*generated* passing/approach chords) — this **IS** the deferred
**Playing-changes Stage 2** (`compileChordTimeline`); bar-lock becomes the trivial case. Everything
rides it.

**Primitive registries:** `COMP_GROOVES` (per-hit target/artic incl. **mute-chug/arpeggiate/swell/
pump/roll/arrastre**, **per-beat `slots`** = the country keystone, `arpPattern` note-order,
`cellBars`/`cellBeats`, **`compLanes[]` ≥2 concurrent lanes**, `couple/unison`) · `BASS_FIGURES`
(incl. **generated** `motown_counter`/`walking` reusing Connect, the **`tresillo` 3-3-2 atom**,
`808_glide`, `connectBass` walk-up) · genre `DRUM_GROOVES` (+ride/rim/openHat/bell lanes, **fills**,
seeded kit-gated humanization, `drums:none`/percussion-role comp) · **voice-leading between backing
chords** + `voicingStyle` {tertian|quartal|shell|drop2|rootless|drone} + `chromatic_mediant` ·
per-lane/per-recipe **swing + swing-LOCK + per-voice split** + half/double-time + swung-16ths +
triplet-subdiv. **Lifelike = GESTURE not timbre** — a per-hit **envelope layer on the existing WAF
sampler** (ZERO new assets) + **kill the sustained pad** (sound-design's #1 fix). `STYLE_PALETTES`
become thin **recipes** over the registries (adding a genre = pick ~5 primitives, zero new code;
startup guard mirrors no-unison).

**Build order v2 (2026-06-05 — supersedes the original §7 order; full detail in the doc's
"Build-plan v2" addendum):** **0** rolling-window scheduler (§14 — ≤50ms play-press, ≤2k live
nodes typical; `_ptStreak` wrap-reset rides along) → **1** finish `chart.timeline` (sub-bar
`durBeats`, `push` clamped at count-in/loop seam, `bass` override, approach tags; keyCycle +
per-block session assembly fixes; determinism assert + the new `smoke-backing-engine.mjs` land
here) → **2** voice-leading between backing chords (thread `prevVoicing`, piano's comper rule-set,
in-voicer hand-span/low-interval guards; modal-M1 tokens + funk-Dorian ride along) → **3**
`COMP_GROOVES` (unified grammar) + pad-kill + mix-7a + `backingDensity` + player-is-the-comp
suppression; boogie migrates to a recipe as the proof → **3.5** mix-7b (shared reverb/pan/carve —
before drums) → **4** `BASS_FIGURES` (root-on-1 kick-locked; boogie = figure #1; walking + motown
generators) → **5** genre `DRUM_GROOVES` + fills same batch (lib/drums.py rename first; seeded
humanize) → **6** palette-as-recipe refactor + guard, then the remaining 8 genres' recipes (each
vetted by its genre-idiom agent) before release → **DEFER behind proof:** `compLanes[]` multi-lane
(reggae bubble, afrobeat interlock, bluegrass roll), multi-bar/polymeter cells (`cellBeats` — Latin
clave, flamenco compás, prog unison), swung-16ths (`swingUnit`), the exotic articulations +
passing-chord generator + quartal/drop2 + `busy_melodic`.

**Discipline (market + L&D): right thing, RIGHT order.** NOW = unbreak the ~9 taught genres +
voice-leading (the proof-loop payload). DEFER = palette breadth + the exotic-meter lanes. **Proof
metric** = seam guide-tone-landing + drill→Jam return-rate (already instrumented via Connect), NOT
minutes-jammed — and it **gates** the breadth tier. **L&D payoff order:** harmonic-rhythm >
voice-leading > comp-grooves > basslines > drums > breadth. Dovetails with **Modal M7/M9** (give
`modal_vamp` a comp/backing layer; sparse modal comp + slow harmonic rhythm) and **Drums Phase D5/D6**
(humanization + genre grooves) below — same registries.

## 🎼 Modal Harmony & Modal Progressions — full-panel audit + To-Do (2026-06-02)

15-agent panel (harmony-theory **CHAIR** + learning-design + guitar/bass/piano-pedagogy + 10 broad genre-idiom agents — jazz/rock/funk/prog/blues/country/classical/metal/pop/latin; subgenre agents excluded per Christian). Q: are we accounting for modal harmony/progressions in everything built so far? **Verdict: PARTIAL** — modal SCALES ✅ complete; harmony ENGINE ✅ already modally correct (`DIATONIC_QUALITIES` has per-mode quality rows; modal vamps produce characteristic chords; **no functional-V7 smuggling** — a modal vamp has no degree-5 to functionalize); but modal HARMONY-as-content is half-built and modal VOCABULARY is barely taught. Full per-lane specs in `.claude/agent-memory/<agent>/`; durable synthesis in memory `project_modal_harmony_audit`. (`COMMON_PROGRESSIONS` has ~28 keys, not 17 — `static_i`/`minor_ii_V_i`/`rhythm_changes_a`/`quick_change_blues` live there; no second table.)

**The gaps (cross-panel consensus):**
- Only the **dark/minor** modal family ships (Aeolian `i-♭VII-♭VI`, Phrygian-metal); the **bright** family (Mixolydian `I-♭VII-IV`, Dorian `i-IV`/`i7-IV7`, Lydian `I-II`, So-What/sus, clean Phrygian `I-♭II`) is documented in `docs/theory-progressions.md` but **NOT in `COMMON_PROGRESSIONS`** → `STYLE_PALETTES`/Jam/Custom/Workouts **can't play a Mixolydian groove or a Dorian vamp**.
- Modes taught as neutral **scale shapes**, not **vocabulary** — the characteristic note (Dorian ♮6 / Mixo ♭7 / Lydian ♯4 / Phrygian ♭2) is never emphasized/felt.
- Curriculum arc **upside-down** — the *easy* static-modal ear skill is buried in Advanced `modal_vamp`; the *hard* mode-of-moment "play the changes" is what "modal" means everywhere else.
- **Bass** groove grip modally **inert** (`bassRootGrip` = root/5th/octave, never reads `cfg.scale`) → `scale:'dorian'` on a bass groove is decorative.
- **No quartal/So-What voicing**; no `nonFunctional`/`modalColor` voicing intent (bury the tritone — the inverse of the changes-voicer).
- **prog/classical/latin have no `STYLE_PALETTES` entry** (no Jam; classical palette-less by design).
- `modal_vamp` routes to `buildScaleExercise` (bare run + drone, **no comp/backing layer**).

**Per-genre #1 modal gap:** jazz=Dorian So-What/Impressions m7 vamp + sus-vamp · rock=Mixolydian `I-♭VII-IV` · funk=Dorian `i7-`**`IV7`** (IV7 carries the ♮6; `static_i` is a bare drone) · blues=static dom7 "Mixolydian-is-home" vamp + minor-blues Dorian (♭7-as-home) · country=Mixolydian ♭VII "train chord" (else country == pop) · pop=Aeolian `i-♭VI-♭III-♭VII` dark loop · prog=no palette + Lydian `I-II` + modal interchange · classical=Phrygian cadence + leading-tone-free modal cadences (church-modes étude/counterpoint) · latin=no palette + Dorian montuno (clave-gated) · **metal=STRONGEST, taught as vocabulary** — only add `phrygian_dominant` as a LEAD scale.

**Token trap (rock/country/funk/pop all independently flagged):** the ♭VII/♭II/major-IV must be `{semis:…}` tokens with explicit major/dom7 qualities — a bare degree-7 silently sounds Aeolian. Ship modal vamps `chordOverride:'auto'`, **never `'dom7'`** (only `andalusian` needs `{5:'dom7'}`).

**Phased To-Do (M1–M16):**
- **Phase 0 — engine foundation (KEYSTONE):** **M1 ✅ BUILT (2026-06-02)** — 8 bright-modal progression tokens (`mixolydian_rock`/`mixolydian_vamp`/`dorian_vamp`/`lydian_vamp`/`so_what`/`phrygian_vamp`/`andalusian`/`modal_mixture`) + `PROGRESSION_QUALITY_OVERRIDES.andalusian={5:'dom7'}` in `COMMON_PROGRESSIONS`; bare degrees so the paired mode supplies the quality (Phrygian ♭II pinned `q:'maj'`). Verified by `probe-modal.mjs` (8/8 modal chords correct — anti-trap cases pass: Mixo ♭VII=maj7, Dorian IV=dom7, Phrygian ♭II=maj) + full 9-suite smoke; harmony-theory-architect sign-off GO. **Dormant until M4 wires them** (no palette/dropdown ref yet). · **M2** quartal/So-What voicing primitive (So-What = 3 stacked 4ths + a maj-3rd on top) · **M3** `nonFunctional`/`modalColor` voicing intent (suppress the tritone, omit the leading tone).
- **Phase 1 — wire styles:** **M4** per-genre palette wiring · **M5** add `prog` + `latin` palettes (latin gated on a clave-locked rhythm cell — don't ship "modal chords + a straight click").
- **Phase 2 — feel the mode:** **M6** characteristic-note emphasis pass (within the shape's fret window, no added shift) · **M7** give `modal_vamp` a comp/backing layer · **M8** modal-aware bass grip + Dorian/Mixo/Phrygian static-vamp bass templates (kill the decorative-`scale` trap) · **M9** sparse-sustained modal comp + slow harmonic rhythm (chord change every 4–8 bars).
- **Phase 3 — curriculum:** **M10** static-modal as an ear skill in late Beginner → harmonic concept in Intermediate → Advanced `modal_vamp` reframed to exotic scales · **M11** distinguish static-modal vs play-the-changes; add a Modal-vamp *flavor* to the existing Application Workout role · **M12** verdict-signal engine gap (a characteristic-tone / non-resolution success signal, else modal grades like functional).
- **Phase 4 — content:** **M13** goal-cards NAME the device (jazz "play over a center"; blues "♭7 is home"; country "the ♭VII train chord") · **M14** new/expanded pathways per genre (modal-jazz, Mixolydian rock, Dorian funk, dom7/minor blues, country ♭VII, prog interchange, classical church-modes + Phrygian cadence, latin montuno, dark-pop Aeolian) — each vetted by its idiom + pedagogy agent.
- **Phase 5 — deferred/gated:** **M15** piano modal design (quartal/So-What + `modalColor`) — gated on the piano `hand`/`finger`/`positionContext` schema · **M16** two unbuilt primitives surfaced — modal two-voice counterpoint (classical; `harmonize:true` only does parallel dyads) + the clave-locked rhythm cell (latin).

**Build order:** M1 is the keystone — ship the progression tokens first (harmony's note-spelling sign-off gates everything). Then palettes (M4) for immediate Jam payoff → feel (M6–M8) → curriculum + content. On-mission throughout (it *names the grammar* — gallop, So-What, the ♭VII train chord — not "generate a song"; metal is the proof that modal-as-vocabulary lands). **NEXT (M1 done):** M4 — wire the new tokens into `STYLE_PALETTES` (immediate Jam/Custom payoff) + the Custom progression dropdown, per the per-genre #1 map above; then M2 (quartal voicing) + M6–M8 (feel). When `andalusian` later gets a harmonic-minor/phrygian-dominant pairing, add it to `MINOR_SPELLED_PROGRESSIONS` (harmony's M4 forward-note).

## 🔧 Workout backing/notes/click desync — FIXED (2026-06-02)

User-reported: in multi-block Workouts the backing track drifted off the visual notes + click. **Root cause:** `makeBundle` synthesized ALL backing from ONE cfg (the session's first-block metadata) over the whole duration, while `buildSessionChart` assembles notes+beats **per-block** (own tempo/meter/key + inter-block breaks). Diagnosed with a probe (10 backing events inside a break gap; single-config Pathways/Custom/Jam were clean). 3-agent fix consult (rhythm-meter chair + harmony + sound-design). Memory: `project_workout_backing_desync_fix`.
- **FIX:** backing is now assembled **per-block** in `buildSessionChart` (each block's comp/bass/drums on its own `segCfg`, swung on its own grid in block-local time, offset onto the timeline; the break gap is backing-silent for free). `makeBundle` branches on `chart.backingEvents` — sessions use the pre-assembled per-block backing + skip the global swing; single exercises unchanged. Extracted `swungTime`/`swingNotesBacking` so swing is per-block (the global `applySwingToBundle` warped later blocks against block-1's grid).
- **Follow-on 2 (per-rung):** the rung builders (`buildBpmLadderChart`/`buildKeyCycleChart`) now emit their OWN per-rung backing (built+swung at each rung's tempo/key); `fillBlockToDuration` tiles it; consumers prefer `chart.backingEvents`. Fixes ladder (per-rung tempo) + key-cycle (per-rung key) backing — incl. the **pre-existing single-exercise** key-cycle/ladder case.
- **Guard:** `smoke-session-sync.mjs` (`npm run smoke:sync`; `npm test` is now **10 suites**) — backing tracks per-block/rung tempo+key, silent in the break, single-config unaffected. Harmony bonus: a Dorian/`static_i` block now voices its OWN scale (was inheriting block-1's mode → the M1 modal vamps in a Workout now sound right).
- **RULE (rhythm-meter):** *every timed array must be assembled in the same per-block loop, or it desyncs.* `backingEvents` + swing were the two that had escaped it.
- **Follow-on 1 (DONE — `b4c669a`, shipped in v0.7.1):** a band re-entry fade. harmony+bass+drums now route through a dedicated **backing-group** gain node (click/notes bypass it; Mixer faders stay upstream); `scheduleBackingEnvelope` rides it for a ~18 ms fade-out into each break + a ~18 ms fade-in on the next downbeat (breaks = gaps in `segmentBounds`, scheduled at absolute ctx-time per pass). Single-exercise modes = no-op at unity. The audible result is a play-test item; smoke confirms no throw.

## 🧪 Golden-file regression for the generator core — DESIGNED, DEFERRED (2026-06-02)

4-agent review (harmony-theory + slopsmith-host-expert + rhythm-meter + market-analyst) of Christian's idea: commit reference generator outputs as golden files; a `test` command diffs new output → intentional-vs-regression, protecting the core's stability while the standalone-fork path stays open. **Verdict: SOUND idea, the panel refined it into a genuinely good design — but DEFER behind the proof-loop + the in-flight modal/transport work.** Full synthesis + the build spec in memory `project_golden_file_harness`.

- **Premise fix (unanimous):** the core is **JavaScript** (`generateExercise`/`generateSession` → `{version,session,chart}`), NOT "pure-Python" — `routes.py` is the dormant shell. Golden the JS **chart**.
- **The refined design (build THIS when triggered):**
  - **Boundary that kills the re-bless treadmill:** byte-golden the core **chart** (pre-`makeBundle`); **property-**assert the bundle's feel layer (count-in / swing / `_tail`) — those live downstream of the core, so they fall outside the chart golden automatically.
  - **Snapshot the pitch-CLASS SET, not the MIDI voicing** — locks *what the chord is* (IP) while leaving *where it sits on the neck* (by-ear register) free → near-zero churn on tuning.
  - **Reference set = the RISK surface** (not "C-scale + arp + lick", which just re-tests plumbing the smokes cover): voiceChord maj/min parity, qualities across modes, the **M1 Mixo/Dorian vamp**, a tritone-sub, a **Connect ii–V–I lick**, + a **7/8 (2+2+3) drill** (the keystone time case) + property-asserted count-in / swung / BPM-ladder bundle cases. Share fixtures across pitch+time.
  - **Build, two tiers:** Tier-1 = clone the Playwright/`smoke-core-purity` pattern (ships today but *rides the host → doesn't advance decoupling*). **Tier-2 (the prize)** = ~30-line plain-Node, gated behind a ~5-line seam (guard the IIFE bootstrap's `document` touches + a `globalThis` export — the half-built `__SS_HARNESS__` hook). Goldens live **core-adjacent** (travel with the core into a standalone repo), `--update` flag = an intentional change is a reviewed git diff. Determinism: seed/avoid `Math.random` on the ref path; keep `.toFixed(6)` rounded values.
  - **Complements (≠ overlaps) `smoke-core-purity.mjs`:** purity guards COUPLING ("can it be lifted out"); goldens guard OUTPUT STABILITY ("does the lifted-out core still behave"). Highest value = the safety net **for the extraction diff itself**.
- **Market's dissent (why deferred):** premature infra that presupposes the extraction it protects; no 2nd consumer yet (CLAUDE.md: no standalone scaffolding until one exists); existing smoke + integrity guards already catch player-relevant regressions; re-bless tax bites hardest during the current modal/transport churn; the build slot belongs to the proof-loop (Phase-9 readouts + ~5 players).
- **TRIGGER to build:** when the engine has **stabilized** (modal arc + transport settled) **OR extraction begins** — whichever first; the Tier-2 de-DOM seam is the natural first step of extraction. Optional opportunistic now: the Tier-2 seam alone (~5 lines, reversible, independently useful).

### ⏸️ Transport redesign DESIGN (5-agent charette) — superseded by the BUILT entry above; kept for the rationale.
> **Transport redesign (5-agent charette → Christian: build FULL two-lane).** Length presets made 30-min Workouts common → `drawRulerFrame()` crammed ~700 bar-numbers into fixed width = illegible picket fence. Christian's DAW-authenticity reconciliation (DAW transport = a deliberate "trickle-down" literacy skill) → it's a FALSE tension, go MORE DAW-authentic. **Full spec + the exact window math + build order in memory `project_transport_two_lane_redesign`** (+ 5 agent-memories). Headlines: **(1)** a **scrolling bars|beats WORKING ruler LOCKED to the note renderers' window** (`chartBeatSeconds`+`AHEAD/BEHIND` §6265/6312, playhead fixed ~22% left, bars pixel-aligned with the falling notes, ~7 bars on screen = always legible, no decimation). **(2)** a **whole-session OVERVIEW/marker strip** — role-tinted NAMED segment bands (the DAW arrangement track) from `sections`/`segmentBounds`, carrying loop-AUTHORING (moves here) + click-seek + block-checkpoints (fill by blocks-cleared, never time), decimated bars `[1,2,5,10,25,50,100]`. **+** min:sec readout, TOKENIZE the ruler's raw hex (last un-tokenized surface). ### ⏸️ Workout PACING build (post-Phase-9 charette) — BUILT + 9-suite green, COMMITTED `152db15` (UNPUSHED); Christian play-testing.

>   - **(1) Inter-block BREAK** — between blocks `buildSessionChart` now inserts a count-in for the INCOMING block (count beats `brk:true` + advance offset): `interBlockBreakBars(prev,cur,mode)` = `round(2/barSec)` whole incoming bars (clamp 1–4), **min 2 bars on a technique-class change (`TECH_CLASS` map) or a ≥5-fret position leap** (hand resets); `mode='auto'` skips when adjacent blocks share tempo+meter+technique+region; `'always'`/`'off'` too. UI: **"Breathe between blocks"** toggle (`#slopscale-breathe-toggle` → `_workoutDraft.interBlockBreak`). The break doubles as the per-block verdict beat. Probe `probe-break.mjs` (6 cases). Defaults ON (auto). NOT a universal segue (rejected as low-payoff).
>   - **(2) Length PRESETS** — `#slopscale-length-preset`: As built (default — natural length preserved) · Quick ~10 · Standard ~20 · Woodshed ~30. `applyLengthPreset(session,preset)` distributes a total across blocks **proportional to natural cell duration** (warm-up stays short) via `targetSec`→`fillBlockToDuration`; applied in `onLaunchSession`, readout flips to `≈N min` (a setup PLAN, never a countdown). Re-scopes the "no minutes" lock to drills (Christian's call). Verified: 900s target → 916s build.

>   - **(4) No hard cap** — past ≥10 blocks `renderWorkoutDraft` shows a calm non-blocking note; never gates Launch.
